ACTOR Sanae 31300
{
//$Category "Touhou Characters"
  Tag "Sanae Kochiya"
  Speed 8
  MONSTER
  Health 2500
  Radius 24
  Height 64
  Scale 0.7
  Mass 1000
  MeleeThreshold 64
  MeleeRange 64
  Species "Moriya"
  +DONTHARMSPECIES
  +DONTHARMCLASS
  +LOOKALLAROUND
  +FLOORCLIP
  +DONTFALL
  +BOSS
  +NEVERRESPAWN
  +NORADIUSDMG
  +DONTRIP
  +DONTMORPH
  +AMBUSH
  +QUICKTORETALIATE
  +NOICEDEATH
  DamageFactor "PlayerSpellcard", 0.5
  Painchance 4
  Seesound ""
  Deathsound "touhou/defeat"
  Obituary "%o was miraculously defeated by Sanae."
  var int user_angle;
  var int user_position;
  DropItem "SanaeGreyThaumaturgy"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SANA A 0
	SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,15,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",3322),false)
	SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,15,70)
  Idle:
    SANA BBBCCCDDDEEEFFFGGGHHHAAA 1 A_Look
    Loop
  See:
    SANA AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFFGGGHHH 1 A_Chase
    Loop
  Pain:
	SANA A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0)
	SANA A 0 A_GiveInventory("SanaeBigStarTrigger",1)
    SANA I 4 A_Pain
	SANA JKJI 4
    Goto See
  Melee:
	SNAT A 0 A_Jump(255,"Melee1","Melee2","Melee3","Melee4","Melee5")
  Melee1:
    SNAT JKLM 2 Fast A_FaceTarget
	SNAT N 2 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(40,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	SNAT OPQR 2 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Melee2:
    SNAT STUV 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	SNAT W 4 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(80,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	SNAT XYZ 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Melee3:
    SNA2 AB 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
    SNA2 CD 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	SNA2 E 4 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(70,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	SNA2 FGHI 3 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Melee4:
    SNA2 JKLMN 2 Fast A_FaceTarget
	SNA2 O 3 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(50,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	SNA2 PQRS 2 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Melee5:
    SNA3 ABC 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	SNA3 D 4 Fast A_CustomMeleeAttack(60,"touhou/remi/hit","none")
	SNA3 EFGHI 4 Fast A_FaceTarget
	Goto See
  Missile:
	Goto BigStar

  BigStarEasy:
	SASP A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SanaeNSBigStarEffect",0,0,32,0,0,0,0,0,0)

ACTOR SanaeNSBigStarEffect
{
  +NOINTERACTION
  +CLIENTSIDEONLY
  RenderStyle Add
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SNST A 0
	SNST A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1,1)
	SNST AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFFAAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 Bright A_FadeIn(0.05)
	TNT1 A 0
	Stop
  }
}
ACTOR SanaeNSBigStarEasy
{
  Radius 2
  Speed 24
  fastspeed 30
  Height 4
  damage (8)
  Projectile
  +FORCEXYBILLBOARD
  +RIPPER
  RenderStyle Add
  SeeSound "touhou/fire"
  DeathSound "touhou/hit"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Disappear")
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("SanaeBigStarTrigger",1,"Death")
	SNST A 3 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(0.9)
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Disappear")
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("SanaeBigStarTrigger",1,"Death")
	SNST B 3 Bright A_ScaleVelocity(0.9)
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1,"Disappear")
	SNST A 0 Bright A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("SanaeBigStarTrigger",1,"Death")

ACTOR SanaeGreyThaumaturgy : Sanae
{
  DropItem "SanaeNS2"
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  MinMissileChance 160
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    SANA A 0
	SANA A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	SANA ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
	SANA AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	SNAT A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	SNAT A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SNAT ABCD 5 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6200)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6200,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",3322),true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6200,70)
	SNAT A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,80)
	SNAT A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SNAT A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)

  Idle:
    SANA A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6201)
    SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6201,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",2211),false)
	SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6201,70)
	SANA BBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6201)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6201,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",2211),false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6201,70)
    SANA AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
	SANA A 0 A_Jump(255,"SmallStars","Amulets1","Amulets2","Snakes","MightyWind")
	Goto Amulets1
  }
}

ACTOR SanaeNS3 : Sanae
{
  //DropItem "SanaeStarRitual" //Screw it, I'm not giving her the full name
  DropItem "None"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    SANA A 0
	SANA A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	SANA ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
    SANA A 1 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6203)
    SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6203,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",1100),false)
	SANA A 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6203,70)
	SANA BBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6203)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6203,ACS_NamedExecuteWithResult("BHI_SpellCardsBySkillLevel",1100),false)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6203,70)
    SANA AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Chase
    Loop
  Missile:
	SANA A 0 A_Jump(255,"SmallStars","Amulets1","Amulets2","Snakes","MightyWind")
	Goto Amulets1
  Death:
	SANA L 1 ACS_NamedTerminate("BHI_BossStartAttack",0)
	SANA L 1 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStopAttack",0)
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("EasyMode",1,"LastSpell")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("NormalMode",1,"LastSpell")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("HardMode",1,"StarRitual")
	TNT1 A 0 A_JumpIfInTargetInventory("LunaticMode",1,"StarRitual")
    Goto StarRitual
  StarRitual:
	SANA L 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
    SANA L 0 A_NoBlocking
	SANA L 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire")
	SANA LLLMMMNNN 2 A_FadeOut(0.1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SanaeStarRitual",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_TELEFRAG,0)
	Stop
  LastSpell:
	SANA L 0 A_GiveInventory("BulletDeathTrigger",1)
    SANA L 0 A_NoBlocking
	SANA L 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/nuefire")
	SANA LLLMMMNNN 2 A_FadeOut(0.1)
	TNT1 A 0 A_SpawnItemEx("SanaeDivineWind",0,0,0,0,0,0,0,SXF_TELEFRAG,0)
	Stop
  }
}

ACTOR SanaeStarRitual : Sanae	//"Star Ritual to Call the Godly Winds"
{								//Yeah, that's kind of long.
  +INVULNERABLE
  +NOPAIN
  +MISSILEMORE
  +MISSILEEVENMORE
  MinMissileChance 160
  DropItem "SanaeDivineWind"
  States
  {
  Spawn:
    SANA A 0
	SANA A 0 A_SetTranslucent(0.1)
	SANA ABCDEF 3 A_FadeIn(0.15)
  Idle:
	SANA AAABBBCCCDDDEEEFFF 1 A_Look
	Goto Idle
  See:
	SNAT A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)
	SNAT A 0 A_JumpIfInventory("SpellcardActive",1,"ChaseState")
    SNAT ABCD 5 A_FaceTarget
    TNT1 A 0 Thing_ChangeTID(0,6204)
    TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartAttack",0,6204,1,true)
	TNT1 A 0 ACS_NamedExecute("BHI_BossStartTimer",0,6204,70)
	SNAT A 0 ACS_Execute(602,0,82)
	SNAT A 0 A_PlaySound("touhou/spellcard",0,1.0,0,ATTN_NONE)
	SNAT A 0 A_GiveInventory("SpellcardActive",1)
	SNAT EFGHGFGHGFGH 3 A_FaceTarget
    SNAT I 5 A_FaceTarget
	SNAT A 0 A_UnSetInvulnerable
	SNAT A 0 A_ChangeFlag("NOPAIN",0)
	Goto Missile
  Pain:
	SNAT A 0 A_SetTranslucent(1.0,0)

    SNAT ABCD 5 A_FaceTarget
